**Before you begin**
This project is under heavy development. Structure, tooling, content are being constantly reviewing and improving.
You can join project creation if you have any ideas how to make it better or time to help.

# Public APIs directory
This project is an attempt to categorise and compile information about different public APIs into one place.
It includes APIs description, links to docs, specification, list of SDK and libraries, logo etc.

This list intended to be maintained by wide open source community, so any contributions appreciated.
If you want to add/edit/remove/etc APIs from this list, please see the [contributing guide](CONTRIBUTE.md).

Discuss any topic related to the specific API you can [here](https://github.com/apis-list/apis-list/discussions/categories/apis)

## APIs

### 3D
- [Graphql360](https://github.com/apis-list/apis-list/tree/main/graphql360) - Create and consume 360 degree panoramic tours using a GraphQL API.
- [Kairos](https://github.com/apis-list/apis-list/tree/main/kairos) - Face recognition, emotion analysis and measuring engagement of people in images or videos for any mobile or web application

### 3d
- [Sketchfab API](https://github.com/apis-list/apis-list/tree/main/sketchfab-api) - Request blocked.

### AI & ML
- [AYLIEN](https://github.com/apis-list/apis-list/tree/main/aylien) - AYLIEN Text Analysis API is a package of Natural Language Processing, Information Retrieval and Machine Learning tools for extracting meaning and insight from textual and visual content with ease.
- [Amazon MI API](https://github.com/apis-list/apis-list/tree/main/amazon-mi-api) - Amazon Machine Learning API simplifies the process of making predictions that require lots of expertise around model building, data cleansing and statistical analysis.
- [Aylien Text Analysis](https://github.com/apis-list/apis-list/tree/main/aylien-text-analysis) - Explore AYLIEN’s advanced NLP APIs.
- [Big ML](https://github.com/apis-list/apis-list/tree/main/big-ml) - This page helps you quickly create your first source, dataset, model, and prediction using the BigML API.
- [Clarifai](https://github.com/apis-list/apis-list/tree/main/clarifai) - Whether you have one input or billions, you are only steps away from using AI to power your business applications.
- [Cloud Machine Learning Engine](https://github.com/apis-list/apis-list/tree/main/cloud-machine-learning-engine) - Take your ML projects to production, quickly and cost-effectively.
- [Cloudmersive Natural Language Processing](https://github.com/apis-list/apis-list/tree/main/cloudmersive-natural-language-processing) - About Us Cloudmersive is a leader in Highly Scalable Cloud APIs.
- [Dark Sky](https://github.com/apis-list/apis-list/tree/main/dark-sky) - Weather.
- [Datum Box](https://github.com/apis-list/apis-list/tree/main/datum-box) - Unleash the power of Machine Learning by using the Powerful and Easy-to-Use API of Datumbox
- [Deepcode](https://github.com/apis-list/apis-list/tree/main/deepcode) - 
- [Detect Language](https://github.com/apis-list/apis-list/tree/main/detect-language) - Detects 164 languages.
- [DialogFlow](https://github.com/apis-list/apis-list/tree/main/dialogflow) - Natural Language Interactions for Bots, Applications, Services, and Devices.
- [Football Prediction](https://github.com/apis-list/apis-list/tree/main/football-prediction) - he API supports competitions in over 90 countries and over 140 national leagues.
- [Google Cloud Natural](https://github.com/apis-list/apis-list/tree/main/google-cloud-natural) - Enables easy integration of Google natural language understanding technologies into developer applications.
- [GrünstromIndex](https://github.com/apis-list/apis-list/tree/main/grunstromindex) - The green electricity index shows when a lot of renewable electricity is in the grid and can be used in the household.
- [IBM Watson](https://github.com/apis-list/apis-list/tree/main/ibm-watson) - Build and train models, and create apps, with a trusted AI-infused platform.
- [Imagga Api](https://github.com/apis-list/apis-list/tree/main/imagga-api) - identifies the content of images and videos, classify images based on content, extracts colors, moderates NSFW content.
- [Infermedica API](https://github.com/apis-list/apis-list/tree/main/infermedica-api) - The most advanced Symptom Checker and Patient Triage API.
- [Kairos](https://github.com/apis-list/apis-list/tree/main/kairos) - Face recognition, emotion analysis and measuring engagement of people in images or videos for any mobile or web application
- [LUIS AI](https://github.com/apis-list/apis-list/tree/main/luis-ai) - Language Understanding Intelligent Service offers a fast and effective way of adding language understanding to applications
- [Language Detection](https://github.com/apis-list/apis-list/tree/main/language-detection) - Detect language(s) from pieces of text
- [Lexalytics](https://github.com/apis-list/apis-list/tree/main/semantria) - Flexible natural language processing APIs and complete text analytics platform solutions for data analytics companies and data analyst teams.
- [MeaningCloud](https://github.com/apis-list/apis-list/tree/main/meaningcloud) - Text analysis APIs for topic extraction, sentiment analysis, automatic classification, morphosyntactic analysis, language detection and more.
- [Microsoft Azure Machine Learning API](https://github.com/apis-list/apis-list/tree/main/microsoft-azure-machine-learning-api) - Azure Cognitive Services brings AI within reach of every developer through a family of APIs that don’t require machine-learning expertise.
- [ObjectCut](https://github.com/apis-list/apis-list/tree/main/objectcut) - Automatic background removal real-time service powered by AI.
- [ParallelDots](https://github.com/apis-list/apis-list/tree/main/paralleldots) - ParallelDots AI APIs are the most comprehensive set of document classification and NLP APIs for software developers that provide state-of-the-art accuracy on most common NLP use-cases such as sentiment analysis and emotion detection.
- [Recast.AI](https://github.com/apis-list/apis-list/tree/main/recast-ai) - Log in to our collaborative chatbot software and start building powerful AI bots.
- [Semantira](https://github.com/apis-list/apis-list/tree/main/semantira) - To get started check out Install the SDK.
- [Sentim-API](https://github.com/apis-list/apis-list/tree/main/sentim-api) - herokuapp.
- [SpeechText.AI API](https://github.com/apis-list/apis-list/tree/main/speechtext-ai-api) - Cloud Speech Recognition API.
- [SummarizeBot API](https://github.com/apis-list/apis-list/tree/main/summarizebot-api) - Multilingual summarization, keywords and sentiment analysis, language recognition, article extraction, comments identification, multimedia analysis, image and face recognition solutions.
- [TextRazor](https://github.com/apis-list/apis-list/tree/main/textrazor) - #FreeToUse.
- [This Person Does not Exist](https://github.com/apis-list/apis-list/tree/main/this-person-does-not-exist) - This Person Does Not Exist
- [Time Door](https://github.com/apis-list/apis-list/tree/main/time-door) - Time Door is an API for statistical insights into time series data.
- [Traitify](https://github.com/apis-list/apis-list/tree/main/traitify) - Traitify API documentation and developer portal.
- [Unplugg](https://github.com/apis-list/apis-list/tree/main/unplugg) - Add intelligence to your energy products.
- [VoiceRSS](https://github.com/apis-list/apis-list/tree/main/voicerss) - An API to convert Text to Speech, supporting 15+ major languages.
- [Vuforia](https://github.com/apis-list/apis-list/tree/main/vuforia) - Developers can easily add advanced computer vision functionality to Android, iOS, and UWP apps, to create AR experiences that realistically interact with objects and the environment.
- [Watson Natural Language Understanding](https://github.com/apis-list/apis-list/tree/main/watson-natural-language-understanding) - Provide text, raw HTML, or a public URL and IBM Watson Natural Language Understanding will give you results for the features you request.
- [Wikitude](https://github.com/apis-list/apis-list/tree/main/wikitude) - Powerful augmented reality apps.
- [Wit.ai](https://github.com/apis-list/apis-list/tree/main/wit-ai) - Natural Language Processing
- [Word Associations API](https://github.com/apis-list/apis-list/tree/main/word-associations-api) - Provides service to get associations for a word or phrase.

### API
- [API2Cart](https://github.com/apis-list/apis-list/tree/main/api2cart) - Connect your B2B eCommerce solution with 40+ shopping platforms and marketplaces at once.
- [AudD](https://github.com/apis-list/apis-list/tree/main/audd) - AudD Music Recognition API Docs: how to identify songs in audio using our API
- [BetterDoctor](https://github.com/apis-list/apis-list/tree/main/betterdoctor) - © 2021 BetterDoctor, Inc.
- [Holiday API](https://github.com/apis-list/apis-list/tree/main/holiday-api) - Start developing for free.
- [IP Sidekick](https://github.com/apis-list/apis-list/tree/main/ip-sidekick) - IP Sidekick is an API that returns information about an IP address.
- [IP2Location](https://github.com/apis-list/apis-list/tree/main/ip2location) - IP Address Geolocation to Country, City, Region, Latitude, Longitude, ZIP Code, ISP, Domain, Time Zone, Area Code, Mobile Data, Usage Type, Elevation and so on.
- [Intellexer](https://github.com/apis-list/apis-list/tree/main/intellexer) - Processing (NLP) Service including sentiment analysis, content extraction, and language detection.
- [JSONPlaceholder](https://github.com/apis-list/apis-list/tree/main/jsonplaceholder) - When to use JSONPlaceholder is a free online REST API that you can use whenever you need some fake data.
- [Lexalytics](https://github.com/apis-list/apis-list/tree/main/semantria) - Flexible natural language processing APIs and complete text analytics platform solutions for data analytics companies and data analyst teams.
- [MLScrape](https://github.com/apis-list/apis-list/tree/main/mlscrape) - MLScrape is an API that allows you to scrape data from any online shop without having to maintain your own web scraper - simply send the product URL to our API.
- [Pdfshift ](https://github.com/apis-list/apis-list/tree/main/pdfshift) - An API to convert HTML/CSS documents to PDF.
- [SecurityTrails](https://github.com/apis-list/apis-list/tree/main/securitytrails) - Welcome to SecurityTrails! This page will help you get started.
- [Traitify](https://github.com/apis-list/apis-list/tree/main/traitify) - Traitify API documentation and developer portal.
- [World Trading Data](https://github.com/apis-list/apis-list/tree/main/world-trading-data) - World Trading Data is a worldwide market data provider, for example provide a stock name and dates and get trading data for those.
- [numverify](https://github.com/apis-list/apis-list/tree/main/numverify) - Free, powerful JSON API offering international and national phone number validation and carrier, location and line type lookup for developers and businesses.

### Accounting

### Accounts
- [Bittrex](https://github.com/apis-list/apis-list/tree/main/bittrex) - Bittrex provides a simple and powerful API consisting of REST endpoints for transactional operations and a complementary Websocket service providing streaming market and user data updates
- [Keyserv](https://github.com/apis-list/apis-list/tree/main/keyserv) - SmartQ is an technology company founded in 2017 with the intention of providing innovative tools for the modern world.

### Facial Recognition
